        </div> 
        <h4 class="heading-4">We pair your donation with<br class="visible-lg"> urgent needs</h4> 
        <p><a href="https://www.gofundme.org/"><span style="font-weight: 400">GoFundMe.org</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400">, our 501(c)(3), turns your donation into grants for people and charities in need. </span></p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="cell large-4 pr"> 
        <div class="icon mb2x"> 
        </div> 
        <h4 class="heading-4">See the impact of your donation</h4> 
        <p><span style="font-weight: 400">Well regularly send you stories from the people and charities youve helped so you can see how youve made a difference. </span></p> 
       </div>
